 Post Name: Technical Staff and Operative Number of Posts: 330 Pay Scale: Rs
 7500-22430 / - zyada jaankaree ke lieyaha clic karen
 When you go to eat in the hotel, now you may have to pay more than the maximum retail price (MRP) to buy a bottle of water
 darasal supreme court ne kaha he ki hotel chahen, to ve pani kii bottle ke liye MRP se zyada paise vasuul sakate hai
 The court has said that in this case hotels and restaurants are not bound by MRP
 justise rohinton nariman ne centre sarkaar ke us tark ko nakaar diya, jisamen usne kaha tha ki jo hotel pani kii bottle ke liye tay emarpy se zyada paise vasuulenge, un par jurmaana lagaaya ja saktaa he
 The central government had also talked about sending such hotel owners to jail
 iconomic times kii ek report ke mutabik supreme court ne is tark ko sire se nakaar diya
 According to the report, the Supreme Court said that when a customer goes to a hotel, he does not go to buy only water balls
 vahaan use kai anya suvidhaayen bhi milti hai
 Due to this, he also gets service there
 centre sarkaar ne kaha tha ki MRP se zyada paise vasuulana na sirf graahakon ke hiton ke khilaaf he, balki yah kar chori kaa bhi jariya ban saktaa he
 However, the Federation of Hotels and Restaurants Association rejected the government's claim outright
 usne kaha ki pani kii bottle ke liye emarpy se zyada paise vasuulne se na graahakon ke hiton ko khatra or na hi yah kar chori kaa jariya banegaa

 yah jasoos kuch alag kism kaa cese lenaa chahta he, or tabhi dimpi singh kaa role kar rahi madalsa sharma unke paas apana cese lekar pahunchati he, or samraat pahunch jaataa he shimla

 jasoos 'samraat' smart he, stylish he or iskaa 'seventh sens' kamaal kaa he
 
 
 He seeks logic in everything and reaches the root of the case on the same basis
 
 
 haalanki film main suspence acha he, magar film kii kamazor kadi lagi samraat kii tafteesh, kyonki kahani main detective ke logic or seventh sens ko itnaa bada dikhaa diya he ki kaatil tak yah kaaphi jaldi or aasaani se pahunch jaataa he
 
 
 Many scenes seem old and childish in this affair
 
 
 jaise-jaise film aage badhati he, kai logon ke liye lagata he ki shaayad yah ho saktaa he kaatil, magar kaatil pahunch se dur jaataa rahata he
 
 
 Though the film does not have much entertainment value, it cannot be denied that the film has kept suspense to the end
 
 
 agar aapako jasusi filmein pasand hai to 'samraat and company' ko ek baar dekh sakate hai
 
 
 My rating for this film is - 3 stars
